MTV Raps</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> and at that time she would also make public in an interview that they were engaged. Brown later said that the latter was part of a joke started by one of the hosts of the show Tyrone "T Money" Kelsie "he came up with the marriage idea and then mayhem ensued. After the initial show, the story got so big that an interviewer actually asked Lyte about her "marriage"... and instead of her shooting down the rumor, she went along with it."<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2023)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>  Later it was speculated in the media that for a few years she had a relationship with actress <a href="/wiki/Tichina_Arnold" title="Tichina Arnold">Tichina Arnold</a>. Later these rumors were denied by Arnold.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> In May 2015 some media speculated that Lyte had dated R&amp;B singer <a href="/wiki/Janelle_Monae" class="mw-redirect" title="Janelle Monae">Janelle Monae</a>, but these rumors have not been confirmed by either of them.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In early 2016, she started dating <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marine Corps</a> veteran and entrepreneur John Wyche, after meeting him on <a href="/wiki/Match.com" title="Match.com">Match.com</a>. They announced their engagement in May 2017. "What can I say, except thank you Lord!!!... It's been a long time, this single life, and I thank you all for your prayers and kind words of hope," she wrote in an <a href="/wiki/Instagram" title="Instagram">Instagram</a> post dated January 21, 2017. "God has sent me true love. For all of you waiting on LOVE- don't give up – keep God first and he will see that you meet your match." In August they exchanged their vows during a musical wedding in <a href="/wiki/Montego_Bay" title="Montego Bay">Montego Bay</a>, Jamaica. <a href="/wiki/Reggae" title="Reggae">Reggae</a> Congo bands played as Lyte walked down the aisle, and the couple's friend <a href="/wiki/Kelly_Price" title="Kelly Price">Kelly Price</a> serenaded them during the ceremony. Afterward, an intimate gathering with only close friends and family members was held.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
In August 2020 she filed for a divorce after three years of marriage.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She is an honorary member of <a href="/wiki/Sigma_Gamma_Rho" title="Sigma Gamma Rho">Sigma Gamma Rho</a> sorority.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Awards_and_nominations">Awards and nominations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=MC_Lyte&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Awards and nominations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_accolades">Other accolades</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=MC_Lyte&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Other accolades">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>2006 – <a href="/wiki/Hip_Hop_Honors" title="Hip Hop Honors">VH1 Hip Hop Honors</a> – <b>Honoree</b><sup id="cite_ref-HHH_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HHH-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>2013 – Hip Hop Inaugural Ball – Honored with the Lifetime Achievement<sup id="cite_ref-ib_75-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ib-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>2013 – <a href="/wiki/BET_Hip_Hop_Awards" title="BET Hip Hop Awards">BET Hip Hop Awards</a> –  Honored with the Icon Lifetime Achievement <b>I Am Hip Hop Award</b> for her contributions to hip-hop culture<sup id="cite_ref-BETHH_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BETHH-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>2016 – <a href="/wiki/Harvard_University" title="Harvard University">Harvard University</a> – Hutchins Center for African and African American Research's <a href="/wiki/W._E._B._Du_Bois_Medal" class="mw-redirect" title="W. E. B. Du Bois Medal">W. E. B. Du Bois Medal</a><sup id="cite_ref-hu_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hu-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>2019 – Trumpet Awards – Trail Blazer Award<sup id="cite_ref-ta_92-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ta-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
